Create a Blog in Less Than 20 Minutes</h1> \n<div class=\"entry-content\"><div id=\"tve_flt\" class=\"tve_flt\"><div id=\"tve_editor\" class=\"tve_shortcode_editor\"><div class=\"thrv_paste_content thrv_wrapper tve_empty_dropzone\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0px !important; margin-top: 20px !important;\"><h4 class=\"tve_p_center\" data-web-font=\"Lucida Sans Unicode, Lucida Grande, sans-serif\" style=\"font-family: 'Lucida Sans Unicode', 'Lucida Grande', sans-serif;\"><span class=\"tve_custom_font_size  rft\" style=\"font-size: 38px;\">We've been featured on:</span></h4><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_columns tve_clearfix\">\n<div class=\"tve_colm tve_fic tve_empty_dropzone\"><div style=\"width: 205px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption aligncenter\">\n<span class=\"tve_colm tve_fic tve_lst tve_empty_dropzone\"><div style=\"width: 445px; margin-top: 30px !important;\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Problogger logo\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Problogger-logo.png\" style=\"width: 445px\" width=\"148\" height=\"31\">\n</span>\n</div></div>\n</div><p>My name is Karl and I run MonetizePros.com. I started my first blog almost 7 years ago and the journey has been life-changing for me in dozens of ways. I've made tens of thousands of dollars, lived in many tropical countries (currently Thailand), met hundreds of amazing entrepreneurs and much more.</p><p>​When I first got started it was simply for fun and some side income. I never expected it to turn into such a high-paying career. But, I'm not special - I'm just like you, an average guy.</p><p style=\"margin-top: 10px !important;\">​Now my goal is to help other people who are in the same position I was, start their own blogs. Follow this step-by-step tutorial and I'll show you exactly how to create a blog that'll make you money for years to come and change your life. It's simple.</p><h4 class=\"rft\" style=\"font-size: 30px;\">Why would I want a blog?</h4><p>Okay, okay. Depending on what background you come from, blogging may sound like a waste of time.&nbsp;</p><p>When I talk about blogging, I don't mean filling out your personal journal for others to see. I'm talking about writing high-quality articles on subjects people care about and solving their problems. This kind of blogging is what makes you money.</p><p>Top bloggers are making hundreds of thousands of dollars per year and some of these guys started only a few years back.</p><p>Even if that's not your main motivator, you'll:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul1 tve_green\" style=\"margin-bottom: -20px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\">Build credibility online and establish your expertise</li>\n<li class=\"\">Become a better writer and thinker</li><li class=\"\">Get more client-work</li><li class=\"\">Make your resume stand out</li><li class=\"\">Learn new things</li><li class=\"\">Have a blast while doing it</li>\n</ul>\n</div><p class=\"bold_text tve_p_center\">Do you want to learn how to start a $1,000/month online business?</p><div style=\"width: 230px;\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption aligncenter\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/start-online-business\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" rel=\"\" data-tcb-events=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"\" style=\"width: 230px;\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Learn-More-Button.png\" width=\"230\" height=\"78\"></a>\n</span>\n</div><br class=\"\"><p id=\"\">If you're still not convinced, I recommend you read this post:&nbsp;<a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/blogging/why-start-a-blog/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">46 Reasons You Should Start a Blog Today</a></p><h4 class=\"rft\" style=\"font-size: 35px; margin-top: -20px !important;\">​Read this part carefully</h4><p>I know what you're doing right now. You're making up a million excuses right now to not do this. </p><p><b>STOP.</b></p><p>It may sound like I'm selling \"the dream\" to you, but the truth is, I'm not selling you anything. </p><p>I'm trying to help you out. You're not going to become a millionaire overnight, but this is what you NEED to do if your goal is financial freedom and location independence, with an enjoyable job.</p><p>Here's a small list of things you're worried about right now:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul4 tve_red\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\">Blogging is too expensive!</li>\n<li class=\"\">I don't have the time for this.</li><li class=\"\">No one is ever going to read my blog</li><li class=\"\">I'm not going to make any money</li><li class=\"\">I don't know what to talk about</li><li class=\"\">BLAH BLAH BLAH</li>\n</ul>\n</div><p>Now stop it. Everyone is afraid when they're starting something new and important, but there's nothing to be afraid of.</p><p>This will be an investment of about 13 cents per day for you, it'll take two hours of your time every single week and I'm going to help you out every step of the way.</p><p>I'll show you exactly how to get started, how to publish your first&nbsp;post, how to design the blog, how to monetize it, how to get visitors to it and everything else you'll need to know.</p><p>There's no programming knowledge needed, barely any money and a little bit of time. Just get started!​</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_contents_table tve_ct tve_clearfix tve_update_contents_table tve_orange tve_p_center\" data-tve-style=\"1\" data-columns=\"1\" data-headers=\"h2,h3\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<div class=\"tve_contents_table tve_clearfix\" data-tve-custom-colour=\"36019268\">\n<span class=\"tve_ct_title bold_text rft\" style=\"color: rgb(244, 244, 244); font-size: 30px;\" data-tve-custom-colour=\"95297294\">Table of Contents</span>\n<div class=\"tve_ct_content tve_clearfix\"><div class=\"ct_column\" style=\"width: 100%; min-height: 354px;\"><div class=\"tve_ct_level0\"><a href=\"#how-to-create-a-blog\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">How to Create a Blog in 9 Simple Steps</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#niche-research\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 1) Find your niche</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#choosing-a-cms\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 2) Choose a content management system (CMS)</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#choosing-buying-a-domain-name\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 3) Choosing and buying a domain name</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#choosing-a-webhost\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 4) Choosing a web hosting company</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#web-host-setup\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 5) Setting up your web hosting</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#how-to-install-wordpress\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 6) How to Install WordPress</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#choosing-wordpress-themes\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 7) Choosing a WordPress theme</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#best-wordpress-plugins\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 8) Choosing your WordPress plugins</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#blogging-on-wordpress\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 9) Publishing your first blog post on WordPress</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level0\"><a href=\"#tab-con-54\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Having issues? I'm here to help!</a></div></div></div>\n</div>\n</div></div><div class=\"thrv_paste_content thrv_wrapper tve_empty_dropzone\"><p><strong></strong></p><div class=\"thrv_paste_content thrv_wrapper tve_empty_dropzone\"><h2 class=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 30px !important;\" id=\"how-to-create-a-blog\">How to Start Your Blog in 9 Simple Steps</h2><h3 class=\"\" id=\"niche-research\" style=\"margin-bottom: 30px !important;\">Step 1) Find your niche</h3><p>Before you actually learn to do this, you need to figure out what you’re going to be writing about. One of the key “secrets” to blogging success is choosing a niche (basically a topic) that you have an interest in and most importantly, have the ability to compete in.</p><p>Choose a niche too small and you’ll run out of blog post ideas, make a lot less money and be limited to just that industry. Choose a niche that’s too broad and you’ll probably have a hard time competing and getting any visitors to your blog.</p><p>When you choose a niche, go for one that:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul3 tve_green\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\">You are super interested in</li>\n<li class=\"\">Has an upwards trend</li><li class=\"\">Has more than one monetization opportunity</li><li class=\"\">You've already got knowledge about</li><li class=\"\">Has relatively low competition</li>\n</ul>\n</div><h4 class=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0px !important;\" id=\"tab-con-27\"><strong>Examples of (good) niches:<br><br></strong></h4><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul5 tve_green tve_empty_dropzone\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important; margin-top: -35px !important; margin-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<div class=\"thrv_paste_content thrv_wrapper\"></div>\n<li class=\"\">Deep sea diving</li><li class=\"\">Dirt bike racing</li><li class=\"\">Swimming techniques</li><li class=\"\">First aid training</li><li class=\"\">Bear hunting</li><li class=\"\">Saving for college</li><li class=\"\">Labrador training</li>\n</ul>\n</div><h3 class=\"\" id=\"choosing-a-cms\">Step 2) Choose a content management system (CMS)</h3><p class=\"gr_ver_2\" spellcheck=\"false\">A content management system is <g class=\"gr_ gr_15 gr-alert gr_gramm gr_run_anim Grammar multiReplace\" id=\"15\" data-gr-id=\"15\">the software</g> your website runs on. That’s where you’re going to log into to actually write your posts, change the design, manage the comments and so on.</p><p>We've actually written a very in-depth post about the <a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/blogging/best-blogging-platforms-compared/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">best blogging platforms</a> on the market and compared them all.</p><p>The conclusion was to use WordPress as we'll be doing with this tutorial.​</p><p>Of course, you can use a programming language and code a website from zero, but we’re trying to show you the easy way. There’re hundreds of pre-made content management systems out there that make your life easier.</p><p>There are two super common ways of starting a weblog, one of them is good, the other is bad.</p><p class=\"tve_p_center\"><span class=\"bold_text\">Over 1,000 people have taken our free online course that <br>teaches how to start a niche online business selling Amazon </span><span class=\"bold_text\">products</span><span class=\"bold_text\">.<br></span></p><div style=\"width: 230px;\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption aligncenter\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/start-online-business\" target=\"_blank\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"\" style=\"width: 230px;\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Learn-More-Button.png\" width=\"230\" height=\"78\" title=\"\"></a>\n</span>\n</div><h4 class=\"\" id=\"tab-con-29\"><strong><br>Using an online blogging platform</strong></h4><p>There are a bunch of websites you can register on, such as <a href=\"http://webs.com\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Webs.com</a>, <a href=\"http://weebly.com\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Weebly.com</a>, <a href=\"http://blogger.com\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Blogger.com</a>. There are thousands of free options available and plenty of premium versions out there as well.</p><p>Although free themes are often great, it's hard to find one with extensive functionality that fits your idea of a perfect blog.&nbsp;</p><p>On MonetizePros.com, we use the <a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/genesis-theme\" target=\"_blank\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Genesis theme.</a>&nbsp;Here's why we love it:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul1 tve_green\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\">Great user experience for our readers</li>\n<li class=\"\">Perfectly SEO optimized</li><li class=\"\">Well coded which means no problems</li><li class=\"\">Super easy to customize and build upon</li><li class=\"\">It's responsive (works on mobile devices)</li><li class=\"\">Ridiculously cheap price</li>\n</ul>\n</div><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_button_shortcode tve_centerBtn\" data-tve-style=\"1\">\n<div class=\"tve_btn data-wpel-link=\"internal\">\n<span class=\"tve_left tve_btn_im\">\n<i></i>\n<span class=\"tve_btn_divider\"></span>\n</span>\n<span class=\"tve_btn_txt\">Get the Genesis Theme</span>\n</a>\n</div>\n</div><p>Here's a quick tutorial on how to install a WordPress theme.</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_toggle_shortcode tve_red\">\n<div class=\"tve_faq\">\n<div class=\"tve_faqI\">\n<div class=\"tve_faqB\"><span class=\"tve_not_editable tve_toggle\"></span>\n<h4 class=\"\" id=\"tab-con-70\">Click here to read how to install a WordPress theme</h4>\n</div>\n<div class=\"tve_faqC tve_empty_dropzone\" style=\"display: none;\">\n<p><b><span class=\"bold_text\">Step 1)</span></b> Log in to your WordPress dashboard by going to yourdomain.com/wp-login.php</p><div style=\"width: 320px;\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption aligncenter\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"How-to-install-a-Wordpress-theme\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/How-to-install-a-Wordpress-theme-1.png\" style=\"width: 320px;\" width=\"320\" height=\"445\">\n</span>\n</div><p><span class=\"bold_text\">Step 2) </span>Choose \"Appearance\" from the left-hand menu and click on \"Themes\"</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Navigate-to-themes\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Navigate-to-themes-1.png\" style=\"width: 3358px\" width=\"728\" height=\"406\">\n</span>\n</div><p><span class=\"bold_text\">Step 3)</span> Click \"Add new\" and then in the same place, \"Upload now\"</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Add-new-theme-Wordpress\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Add-new-theme-Wordpress-1.png\" style=\"width: 3358px\" width=\"728\" height=\"416\">\n</span>\n</div><p><span class=\"bold_text\">Step 4)</span> Click on \"Choose file\" and upload your theme (.zip file), click \"Install now\"</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Installing-a-Wordpress-theme\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Installing-a-Wordpress-theme-1.png\" style=\"width: 3358px\" width=\"728\" height=\"416\">\n</span>\n</div><p><span class=\"bold_text\">Step 5) </span>Click on \"Activate\" and your new theme will be live</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Activating-a-Wordpress-theme\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Activating-a-Wordpress-theme-1.png\" style=\"width: 3358px\" width=\"728\" height=\"416\">\n</span>\n</div><p><span class=\"bold_text\">Done!</span> In five simple steps, you've just gotten a brand new website design!</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Brand-new-website-design\" nofollow\">﻿﻿Prolog WordPress theme﻿﻿.</a> It looks like a traditional blog, has a lot of functionality and is mobile responsive.</p><p>Although the theme itself is different, the installation process is the same as in the video above.</p><h3 class=\"\" id=\"best-wordpress-plugins\" style=\"margin-bottom: 30px !important;\">Step 8) Choosing your WordPress plugins</h3><p>WordPress plugins are essentially small apps that you can install on your website to give it more functionality. This could be a plugin that shows popups, collects emails, creates a contact form, redirects links - anything.</p><p>Here are 7 WordPress plugins that we think are must-have:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul6 tve_green\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://sumome.com/partner/monetizepros\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">SumoMe</a> -&nbsp;12+ Free tools to grow your website automatically &amp; make more money</li>\n<li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/wordpress-seo/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Yoast SEO</a> - The easiest way to optimize your website for search engines</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/w3-total-cache/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">W3 Total Cache</a> - Make your website load faster</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/ewww-image-optimizer/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">EWWW Image Optimizer</a> - Automatically compress images to make your website faster</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/updraftplus/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">UpdraftPlus</a> - Automatically create backups of your website</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/wordfence/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Wordfence Security</a> - Prevent hacking attempts, keep your website secure</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/contact-form-7/\" target=\"_blank\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Contact Form 7</a> - The easiest way to let your readers get in touch with you</li>\n</ul>\n</div><p>Here's a video on how-to install a WordPress plugin.</p><div class=\"thrv_responsive_video thrv_wrapper\" data-overlay=\"0\" data-type=\"youtube\" data-embed_type=\"inline\" data-url=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AXM1QgMODW0\" data-embeded-url=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/AXM1QgMODW0\" data-autoplay=\"0\" data-showinfo=\"0\">\n<div class=\"tve_responsive_video_container\" style=\"display: block;\">\n<div class=\"video_overlay\"></div>\n<iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/AXM1QgMODW0?rel=1&amp;modestbranding=0&amp;controls=1&amp;showinfo=0&amp;fs=1&amp;wmode=transparent\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"display: block;\" data-src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/AXM1QgMODW0?rel=1&amp;modestbranding=0&amp;controls=1&amp;showinfo=0&amp;fs=1&amp;wmode=transparent\"></iframe>\n</div>\n</div><h3 class=\"\" id=\"blogging-on-wordpress\" style=\"margin-bottom: 30px !important;\">Step 9) Publishing your first blog post on WordPress</h3><p>Why did you want to know how to create a blog? So you could write a blog post, of course! With WordPress, this is super simple.</p><p>Log in to your admin dashboard at yourdomain.com/wp-login.php/ and choose \"Posts\" and \"Add new\" from the left-hand sidebar.​</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Adding-a-new-post-on-Wordpress\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Adding-a-new-post-on-Wordpress-1.png\" style=\"width: 3358px\" width=\"806\" height=\"460\">\n</span>\n</div><p>Now it's as simple as entering your content and pressing publish!</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Publishing-your-blog-post\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Publishing-your-blog-post-1.png\" style=\"width: 3358px\" width=\"806\" height=\"460\">\n</span>\n</div><p>You now know how to create a blog - congratulations! Want to start another one? Simply go through the process again!</p><h2 class=\"\" id=\"tab-con-54\" style=\"margin-bottom: 30px !important;\">Having issues? Create a Blog in Less Than 20 Minutes</h1> \n<div class=\"entry-content\"><div id=\"tve_flt\" class=\"tve_flt\"><div id=\"tve_editor\" class=\"tve_shortcode_editor\"><div class=\"thrv_paste_content thrv_wrapper tve_empty_dropzone\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0px !important; margin-top: 20px !important;\"><h4 class=\"tve_p_center\" data-web-font=\"Lucida Sans Unicode, Lucida Grande, sans-serif\" style=\"font-family: 'Lucida Sans Unicode', 'Lucida Grande', sans-serif;\"><span class=\"tve_custom_font_size  rft\" style=\"font-size: 38px;\">We've been featured on:</span></h4><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_columns tve_clearfix\">\n<div class=\"tve_colm tve_fic tve_empty_dropzone\"><div style=\"width: 205px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption aligncenter\">\n<span class=\"tve_colm tve_fic tve_empty_dropzone\"><div style=\"width: 528px; margin-top: 25px !important;\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption aligncenter\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"EOFire\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/EOFire.png\" style=\"width: 528px\" width=\"148\" height=\"35\">\n</span>\n</div></div>\n<div class=\"tve_colm tve_fic tve_lst tve_empty_dropzone\"><div style=\"width: 445px; margin-top: 30px !important;\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Problogger logo\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/04/Problogger-logo.png\" style=\"width: 445px\" width=\"148\" height=\"31\">\n</span>\n</div></div>\n</div><p>My name is Karl and I run MonetizePros.com. I started my first blog almost 7 years ago and the journey has been life-changing for me in dozens of ways. I've made tens of thousands of dollars, lived in many tropical countries (currently Thailand), met hundreds of amazing entrepreneurs and much more.</p><p>​When I first got started it was simply for fun and some side income. I never expected it to turn into such a high-paying career. But, I'm not special - I'm just like you, an average guy.</p><p style=\"margin-top: 10px !important;\">​Now my goal is to help other people who are in the same position I was, start their own blogs. Follow this step-by-step tutorial and I'll show you exactly how to create a blog that'll make you money for years to come and change your life. It's simple.</p><h4 class=\"rft\" style=\"font-size: 30px;\">Why would I want a blog?</h4><p>Okay, okay. Depending on what background you come from, blogging may sound like a waste of time.&nbsp;</p><p>When I talk about blogging, I don't mean filling out your personal journal for others to see. I'm talking about writing high-quality articles on subjects people care about and solving their problems. This kind of blogging is what makes you money.</p><p>Top bloggers are making hundreds of thousands of dollars per year and some of these guys started only a few years back.</p><p>Even if that's not your main motivator, you'll:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul1 tve_green\" style=\"margin-bottom: -20px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\">Build credibility online and establish your expertise</li>\n<li class=\"\">Become a better writer and thinker</li><li class=\"\">Get more client-work</li><li class=\"\">Make your resume stand out</li><li class=\"\">Learn new things</li><li class=\"\">Have a blast while doing it</li>\n</ul>\n</div><p class=\"bold_text tve_p_center\">Do you want to learn how to start a $1,000/month online business?</p><div style=\"width: 230px;\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption aligncenter\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/start-online-business\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" rel=\"\" data-tcb-events=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"\" style=\"width: 230px;\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Learn-More-Button.png\" width=\"230\" height=\"78\"></a>\n</span>\n</div><br class=\"\"><p id=\"\">If you're still not convinced, I recommend you read this post:&nbsp;<a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/blogging/why-start-a-blog/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">46 Reasons You Should Start a Blog Today</a></p><h4 class=\"rft\" style=\"font-size: 35px; margin-top: -20px !important;\">​Read this part carefully</h4><p>I know what you're doing right now. You're making up a million excuses right now to not do this. </p><p><b>STOP.</b></p><p>It may sound like I'm selling \"the dream\" to you, but the truth is, I'm not selling you anything. </p><p>I'm trying to help you out. You're not going to become a millionaire overnight, but this is what you NEED to do if your goal is financial freedom and location independence, with an enjoyable job.</p><p>Here's a small list of things you're worried about right now:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul4 tve_red\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\">Blogging is too expensive!</li>\n<li class=\"\">I don't have the time for this.</li><li class=\"\">No one is ever going to read my blog</li><li class=\"\">I'm not going to make any money</li><li class=\"\">I don't know what to talk about</li><li class=\"\">BLAH BLAH BLAH</li>\n</ul>\n</div><p>Now stop it. Everyone is afraid when they're starting something new and important, but there's nothing to be afraid of.</p><p>This will be an investment of about 13 cents per day for you, it'll take two hours of your time every single week and I'm going to help you out every step of the way.</p><p>I'll show you exactly how to get started, how to publish your first&nbsp;post, how to design the blog, how to monetize it, how to get visitors to it and everything else you'll need to know.</p><p>There's no programming knowledge needed, barely any money and a little bit of time. Just get started!​</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_contents_table tve_ct tve_clearfix tve_update_contents_table tve_orange tve_p_center\" data-tve-style=\"1\" data-columns=\"1\" data-headers=\"h2,h3\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<div class=\"tve_contents_table tve_clearfix\" data-tve-custom-colour=\"36019268\">\n<span class=\"tve_ct_title bold_text rft\" style=\"color: rgb(244, 244, 244); font-size: 30px;\" data-tve-custom-colour=\"95297294\">Table of Contents</span>\n<div class=\"tve_ct_content tve_clearfix\"><div class=\"ct_column\" style=\"width: 100%; min-height: 354px;\"><div class=\"tve_ct_level0\"><a href=\"#how-to-create-a-blog\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">How to Create a Blog in 9 Simple Steps</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#niche-research\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 1) Find your niche</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#choosing-a-cms\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 2) Choose a content management system (CMS)</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#choosing-buying-a-domain-name\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 3) Choosing and buying a domain name</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#choosing-a-webhost\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 4) Choosing a web hosting company</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#web-host-setup\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 5) Setting up your web hosting</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#how-to-install-wordpress\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 6) How to Install WordPress</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#choosing-wordpress-themes\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 7) Choosing a WordPress theme</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#best-wordpress-plugins\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 8) Choosing your WordPress plugins</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level1\"><a href=\"#blogging-on-wordpress\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Step 9) Publishing your first blog post on WordPress</a></div><div class=\"tve_ct_level0\"><a href=\"#tab-con-54\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Having issues? I'm here to help!</a></div></div></div>\n</div>\n</div></div><div class=\"thrv_paste_content thrv_wrapper tve_empty_dropzone\"><p><strong></strong></p><div class=\"thrv_paste_content thrv_wrapper tve_empty_dropzone\"><h2 class=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 30px !important;\" id=\"how-to-create-a-blog\">How to Start Your Blog in 9 Simple Steps</h2><h3 class=\"\" id=\"niche-research\" style=\"margin-bottom: 30px !important;\">Step 1) Find your niche</h3><p>Before you actually learn to do this, you need to figure out what you’re going to be writing about. One of the key “secrets” to blogging success is choosing a niche (basically a topic) that you have an interest in and most importantly, have the ability to compete in.</p><p>Choose a niche too small and you’ll run out of blog post ideas, make a lot less money and be limited to just that industry. Choose a niche that’s too broad and you’ll probably have a hard time competing and getting any visitors to your blog.</p><p>When you choose a niche, go for one that:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul3 tve_green\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\">You are super interested in</li>\n<li class=\"\">Has an upwards trend</li><li class=\"\">Has more than one monetization opportunity</li><li class=\"\">You've already got knowledge about</li><li class=\"\">Has relatively low competition</li>\n</ul>\n</div><h4 class=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0px !important;\" id=\"tab-con-27\"><strong>Examples of (good) niches:<br><br></strong></h4><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul5 tve_green tve_empty_dropzone\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important; margin-top: -35px !important; margin-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<div class=\"thrv_paste_content thrv_wrapper\"></div>\n<li class=\"\">Deep sea diving</li><li class=\"\">Dirt bike racing</li><li class=\"\">Swimming techniques</li><li class=\"\">First aid training</li><li class=\"\">Bear hunting</li><li class=\"\">Saving for college</li><li class=\"\">Labrador training</li>\n</ul>\n</div><h3 class=\"\" id=\"choosing-a-cms\">Step 2) Choose a content management system (CMS)</h3><p class=\"gr_ver_2\" spellcheck=\"false\">A content management system is <g class=\"gr_ gr_15 gr-alert gr_gramm gr_run_anim Grammar multiReplace\" id=\"15\" data-gr-id=\"15\">the software</g> your website runs on. That’s where you’re going to log into to actually write your posts, change the design, manage the comments and so on.</p><p>We've actually written a very in-depth post about the <a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/blogging/best-blogging-platforms-compared/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">best blogging platforms</a> on the market and compared them all.</p><p>The conclusion was to use WordPress as we'll be doing with this tutorial.​</p><p>Of course, you can use a programming language and code a website from zero, but we’re trying to show you the easy way. There’re hundreds of pre-made content management systems out there that make your life easier.</p><p>There are two super common ways of starting a weblog, one of them is good, the other is bad.</p><p class=\"tve_p_center\"><span class=\"bold_text\">Over 1,000 people have taken our free online course that <br>teaches how to start a niche online business selling Amazon </span><span class=\"bold_text\">products</span><span class=\"bold_text\">.<br></span></p><div style=\"width: 230px;\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption aligncenter\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/start-online-business\" target=\"_blank\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"\" style=\"width: 230px;\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Learn-More-Button.png\" width=\"230\" height=\"78\" title=\"\"></a>\n</span>\n</div><h4 class=\"\" id=\"tab-con-29\"><strong><br>Using an online blogging platform</strong></h4><p>There are a bunch of websites you can register on, such as <a href=\"http://webs.com\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Webs.com</a>, <a href=\"http://weebly.com\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Weebly.com</a>, <a href=\"http://blogger.com\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Blogger.com</a>. Then you have to hire a separate person, a developer, to put that design into code and make it functional. With WordPress, all of these extra expenses are eliminated. WordPress has themes.</p><p>A WordPress theme is basically a pre-made design for your website that takes only one click to install and one click to activate - you can change this as many times as you wish, as often as you wish. This way you can have a website in any kind of style, with any kind of purpose in a super short amount of time, with no technical knowledge needed.</p><p>The default WordPress theme is not very impressive, that’s why we’re going to show you how to change it. There are thousands of free options available and plenty of premium versions out there as well.</p><p>Although free themes are often great, it's hard to find one with extensive functionality that fits your idea of a perfect blog.&nbsp;</p><p>On MonetizePros.com, we use the <a href=\"https://monetizepros.com/genesis-theme\" target=\"_blank\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Genesis theme.</a>&nbsp;Here's why we love it:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul1 tve_green\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\">Great user experience for our readers</li>\n<li class=\"\">Perfectly SEO optimized</li><li class=\"\">Well coded which means no problems</li><li class=\"\">Super easy to customize and build upon</li><li class=\"\">It's responsive (works on mobile devices)</li><li class=\"\">Ridiculously cheap price</li>\n</ul>\n</div><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_button_shortcode tve_centerBtn\" data-tve-style=\"1\">\n<div class=\"tve_btn data-wpel-link=\"internal\">\n<span class=\"tve_left tve_btn_im\">\n<i></i>\n<span class=\"tve_btn_divider\"></span>\n</span>\n<span class=\"tve_btn_txt\">Get the Genesis Theme</span>\n</a>\n</div>\n</div><p>Here's a quick tutorial on how to install a WordPress theme.</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_toggle_shortcode tve_red\">\n<div class=\"tve_faq\">\n<div class=\"tve_faqI\">\n<div class=\"tve_faqB\"><span class=\"tve_not_editable tve_toggle\"></span>\n<h4 class=\"\" id=\"tab-con-70\">Click here to read how to install a WordPress theme</h4>\n</div>\n<div class=\"tve_faqC tve_empty_dropzone\" style=\"display: none;\">\n<p><b><span class=\"bold_text\">Step 1)</span></b> Log in to your WordPress dashboard by going to yourdomain.com/wp-login.php</p><div style=\"width: 320px;\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption aligncenter\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" height=\"445\">\n</span>\n</div><p><span class=\"bold_text\">Step 2) </span>Choose \"Appearance\" from the left-hand menu and click on \"Themes\"</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Navigate-to-themes\" class=\"bold_text\">Step 3)</span> Click \"Add new\" and then in the same place, \"Upload now\"</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Add-new-theme-Wordpress\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Add-new-theme-Wordpress-1.png\" now\"</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Installing-a-Wordpress-theme\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Installing-a-Wordpress-theme-1.png\" style=\"width: 3358px\" width=\"728\" height=\"416\">\n</span>\n</div><p><span is the same as in the video above.</p><h3 class=\"\" id=\"best-wordpress-plugins\" style=\"margin-bottom: 30px !important;\">Step 8) Choosing your WordPress plugins</h3><p>WordPress plugins are essentially small apps that you can install on your website to give it more functionality. This could be a plugin that shows popups, collects emails, creates a contact form, redirects links - anything.</p><p>Here are 7 WordPress plugins that we think are must-have:</p><div class=\"thrv_wrapper thrv_bullets_shortcode\">\n<ul class=\"tve_ul tve_ul6 tve_green\" style=\"padding-bottom: 0px !important;\">\n<li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://sumome.com/partner/monetizepros\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">SumoMe</a> -&nbsp;12+ Free tools to grow your website automatically &amp; make more money</li>\n<li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/wordpress-seo/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Yoast SEO</a> - The easiest way to optimize your website for search engines</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/w3-total-cache/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">W3 Total Cache</a> - Make your website load faster</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/ewww-image-optimizer/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">EWWW Image Optimizer</a> - Automatically compress images to make your website faster</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/updraftplus/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">UpdraftPlus</a> - Automatically create backups of your website</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/wordfence/\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Wordfence Security</a> - Prevent hacking attempts, keep your website secure</li><li class=\"\"><a href=\"https://wordpress.org/plugins/contact-form-7/\" target=\"_blank\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer nofollow\">Contact Form 7</a> - The easiest way to let your readers get in touch with you</li>\n</ul>\n</div><p>Here's a video on how-to install a WordPress plugin.</p><div class=\"thrv_responsive_video thrv_wrapper\" data-overlay=\"0\" data-type=\"youtube\" data-embed_type=\"inline\" data-url=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AXM1QgMODW0\" data-embeded-url=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/AXM1QgMODW0\" data-autoplay=\"0\" data-showinfo=\"0\">\n<div class=\"tve_responsive_video_container\" style=\"display: block;\">\n<div class=\"video_overlay\"></div>\n<iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/AXM1QgMODW0?rel=1&amp;modestbranding=0&amp;controls=1&amp;showinfo=0&amp;fs=1&amp;wmode=transparent\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"\" style=\"display: block;\" data-src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/AXM1QgMODW0?rel=1&amp;modestbranding=0&amp;controls=1&amp;showinfo=0&amp;fs=1&amp;wmode=transparent\"></iframe>\n</div>\n</div><h3 class=\"\" id=\"blogging-on-wordpress\" style=\"margin-bottom: 30px !important;\">Step 9) Publishing your first blog post on WordPress</h3><p>Why did you want to know how to create a blog? So you could write a blog post, of course! With WordPress, this is super simple.</p><p>Log in to your admin dashboard at yourdomain.com/wp-login.php/ and choose \"Posts\" and \"Add new\" from the left-hand sidebar.​</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Adding-a-new-post-on-Wordpress\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Adding-a-new-post-on-Wordpress-1.png\" style=\"width: 3358px\" width=\"806\" height=\"460\">\n</span>\n</div><p>Now it's as simple as entering your content and pressing publish!</p><div style=\"width: 3358px\" class=\"thrv_wrapper tve_image_caption\">\n<span class=\"tve_image_frame\">\n<img class=\"tve_image\" alt=\"Publishing-your-blog-post\" src=\"https://d1aqjv7vyrf1tv.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Publishing-your-blog-post-1.png\" style=\"width: 3358px\" width=\"806\" height=\"460\">\n</span>\n</div><p>You now know how to create a blog - congratulations!
